Bolton was contemplating?\nOn April 10, 2018, Homeland Security Advisor Tom Bossert resigned at John R. Bolton's request, and John R. Bolton said he was considering a merger of the NSC with the Homeland Security Council."], ['Tom Bossert', 'Thomas P. "Tom" Tom Bossert (born March 25, 1975) is an American lawyer and Republican White House staffer, currently serving President Donald Trump as Homeland Security Advisor. Immediately before, he was fellow at the Atlantic Council and prior to that he served as Deputy Homeland Security Advisor to President George W. Bush. In that capacity, he co-authored the 2007 National Strategy for Homeland Security. Prior to that, Tom Bossert held positions in the Federal Emergency Management Agency, the Small Business Administration, the Office of the Independent Counsel, and the House of Representatives. He also was appointed as the Director of Infrastructure Protection under Bush, overseeing the security of critical U.S. infrastructure, a post he held for two years. Following that, he was appointed the Senior Director for Preparedness Policy within the Executive Office of the President.']]]

"Tom" Tom Bossert (born March 25, 1975) is an American lawyer and Republican White House staffer, currently serving President Donald Trump as Homeland Security Advisor. Immediately before, he was fellow at the Atlantic Council and prior to that he served as Deputy Homeland Security Advisor to President George W. Bush. In that capacity, he co-authored the 2007 National Strategy for Homeland Security. Prior to that, Tom Bossert held positions in the Federal Emergency Management Agency, the Small Business Administration, the Office of the Independent Counsel, and the House of Representatives. He also was appointed as the Director of Infrastructure Protection under Bush, overseeing the security of critical U.S. infrastructure, a post he held for two years. Following that, he was appointed the Senior Director for Preparedness Policy within the Executive Office of the President.']], [['National Security Homeland', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Homeland Security', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Trump', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Homeland', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Tom Bossert', 'Thomas P. "Tom" Tom Bossert (born March 25, 1975) is an American lawyer and Republican White House staffer, currently serving President Donald Trump as Homeland Security Advisor. "Tom" Tom Bossert (born March 25, 1975) is an American lawyer and Republican White House staffer, currently serving President Donald Trump as Homeland Security Advisor. Immediately before, he was fellow at the Atlantic Council and prior to that he served as Deputy Homeland Security Advisor to President George W. Bush. In that capacity, he co-authored the 2007 National Strategy for Homeland Security. Prior to that, Tom Bossert held positions in the Federal Emergency Management Agency, the Small Business Administration, the Office of the Independent Counsel, and the House of Representatives. He also was appointed as the Director of Infrastructure Protection under Bush, overseeing the security of critical U.S. infrastructure, a post he held for two years. Following that, he was appointed the Senior Director for Preparedness Policy within the Executive Office of the President.']], [['National Security Homeland', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Homeland Security', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Trump', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Homeland', 'What rank Trump administration elevated the Home to?\nAt the start of the Trump administration, the position of Homeland, occupied by Tom Bossert, was elevated to the rank of Assistant to the President, making it equal in rank to the National Security Homeland.'], ['Tom Bossert', 'Thomas P. "Tom" Tom Bossert (born March 25, 1975) is an American lawyer and Republican White House staffer, currently serving President Donald Trump as Homeland Security Advisor. In that capacity, he co-authored the 2007 National Strategy for Homeland Security. "Tom" Tom Bossert (born March 25, 1975) is an American lawyer and Republican White House staffer, currently serving President Donald Trump as Homeland Security Advisor. In that capacity, he co-authored the 2007 National Strategy for Homeland Security.
